class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-2834f1cd elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="2834f1cd" data-element_type="section">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class="elementor-row">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-b9c7942" data-id="b9c7942" data-element_type="column">\n\t\t\t<div class="elementor-column-wrap data-id="224f1788" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">\n\t\t\t\t<div class="elementor-widget-container">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix"><p><!-- wp:html --></p>\r\n<p>For more than 20 years, UCI\xe2\x80\x99s <strong>Department of Statistics</strong> has continued to grow as a leader in creating statistical methodology for use in data science applications. With an emphasis on research in statistical theory and interdisciplinary collaborations, the department has grown over the years to house the Center for Statistical Consulting, providing statistical expertise through collaborative relationships with researchers across the campus and community, and was one of the first in the world to offer an undergraduate degree in data science. Explore the statistics website to learn more about our accomplishments and how you can become part of our community.</p>\r\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p><strong>Job Opportunities</strong><br />For a listing of current academic positions open in the Statistics Department, visit the <a href="https://recruit.ap.uci.edu/apply#donald-bren-school-of-information-and-computer-sciences">Academic Recruitment website</a>.</p>\r\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\r\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\r\n<!--\r\n<p><strong>Fall 2023 Seminar Series</strong></p>\r\n<p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" vspace="8" /> June 2 at 4 p.m.<br /><strong>Mine Dogucu</strong><br />Assistant Professor of Teaching, Department of Statistics, UCI<a /></p>\r\n<p style="margin-top: 1em;"><a href="/seminar-series/">Spring 2022 Seminar Schedule</a></p>\r\n<p><!-- /wp:html -->\r\n<p><!-- wp:paragraph --></p>\r\n<p><!-- /wp:paragraph class="entry-content front-copy">\n\t\t\t<p><img decoding="async" width="1600" height="153" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-329" alt="informatics-is-everywhere-2x" src="http://www.informatics.uci.edu/wp-content/uploads/informatics-is-everywhere-2x.png" srcset="https://www.informatics.uci.edu/wp-content/uploads/informatics-is-everywhere-2x.png 1600w, https://www.informatics.uci.edu/wp-content/uploads/informatics-is-everywhere-2x-300x28.png 300w, https://www.informatics.uci.edu/wp-content/uploads/informatics-is-everywhere-2x-1024x97.png 1024w, https://www.informatics.uci.edu/wp-content/uploads/informatics-is-everywhere-2x-624x59.png 624w" sizes="(max-width: 1600px) 100vw, 1600px" /><br />\n<p style="font-family: Times, Hoefler Text, Utopia, Liberation Serif, Nimbus Roman No9 L, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 20px; line-height: 1.4em;">Informatics. It\xe2\x80\x99s the field you\xe2\x80\x99ve never heard of, and the one you know everything about. In a digital age, technology \xe2\x80\x94 how we design it, how we use it and how it affects us \xe2\x80\x94 touches all aspects of our lives. It shapes the way we live, the way we work and the way we build the foundations of a global society. Informatics is a window into this dynamic relationship, examining the interplay of people and technology and what it means for our collective future.</p>\n\t\t</div>\n\n\n\t\t</div><!-- #content -->\n\t</div><!-- #primary -->\n\n\t</div><!-- #main .wrapper -->\n\t<footer id="colophon" role="contentinfo" class="group">\n\t\t\n\t\t<div id="footer_extras">\n\t\t\t<div class="menu-very-top-footer-container"><ul id="menu-very-top-footer" class="menu"><li id="menu-item-429" class="menu-item menu-item-type-post_type menu-item-object-page menu-item-429"><a href="https://www.informatics.uci.edu/people/">People</a></li>\n<li id="menu-item-428" class="menu-item menu-item-type-post_type menu-item-object-page menu-item-428"><a href="https://www.informatics.uci.edu/contact/">Contact</a></li>\n<li id="menu-item-427" class="menu-item menu-item-type-post_type menu-item-object-page menu-item-427"><a href="https://www.informatics.uci.edu/site-map/">Site Map</a></li>\n<li id="menu-item-424" class="menu-item menu-item-type-post_type menu-item-object-page menu-item-424"><a href="https://www.informatics.uci.edu/very-top-footer-menu-items/news/">News</a></li>\n</ul></div>\t\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t<div class="group">\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div id="bren">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href="http://www.ics.uci.edu/"><img src="https://www.informatics.uci.edu/wp-content/themes/informatics/i/DBren_InfoCompSc_logo-UPDATED.png"></a>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div class="site-info">\n\t\t\t\t\t<!-- Display Footer Menu -->\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class="menu-footer-links-container"><ul id="menu-footer-links" class="menu"><li id="menu-item-1220" class="menu-item menu-item-type-custom menu-item-object-custom menu-item-1220"><a href="mailto:ichair@ics.uci.edu">Feedback</a></li>\n<li id="menu-item-1221" class="menu-item menu-item-type-custom menu-item-object-custom menu-item-1221"><a href="http://uci.edu/privacy/">Privacy Policy</a></li>\n</ul></div>\t\t\t\t\t&copy;
